);

    subscription_status BOOLEAN
);

    date_created TIMESTAMP
);</t><s>INSERT INTO marketing_campaigns (campaign_id, campaign_name, start_date, end_date, budget) VALUES ('d1b4210c-4e97-4dd0-bf9b-2fb147e9bb9b', 'Summer Sale Campaign', '2023-07-01', '2023-08-31', 50000.00);</s>

    customer_name TEXT,
    email TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE interactions (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT,
    ad_id INT,
    interaction_type TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE ads (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    campaign_id INT,
    ad_content TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE campaigns (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    campaign_name TEXT,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE
);</t><s>INSERT INTO campaigns(id, campaign_name, start_date, end_date) VALUES (1, 'Campaign 1', '2022-01-01', '2022-12-31');</s>
